<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">THIS PROXY IS SOLICITED ON BEHALF OF THE BOARD OF
DIRECTORS<br>
FOR THE ANNUAL MEETING OF SHAREHOLDERS TO BE HELD ON APRIL&nbsp;24, 2003</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The undersigned shareholder of Apple
Computer, Inc., a California corporation, hereby acknowledges receipt of the
Notice of Annual Meeting of Shareholders and Proxy Statement with respect</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">  </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">to the Annual Meeting of Shareholders of Apple Computer, Inc. to be held
at 1 Infinite Loop, Cupertino, California 95014 on Thursday, April&nbsp;24,
2003 at 10:00&nbsp;a.m., and hereby appoints</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">  </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Fred&nbsp;D.
Anderson and Nancy&nbsp;R. Heinen, and each of them, proxies and attorneys-in-fact,
each with power of substitution and revocation, and each with all powers that
the undersigned would</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">  </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">possess if
personally present, to vote the Apple Computer, Inc. Common Stock of the
undersigned at such meeting and any postponements or adjournments of such
meeting, as set forth below,</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">  </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">and
in their discretion upon any other business that may properly come before the
meeting (and any such postponements or adjournments).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">THIS PROXY WILL BE VOTED AS
SPECIFIED OR, IF NO CHOICE IS SPECIFIED, FOR THE ELECTION OF THE NOMINEES, FOR
PROPOSALS 2, 3, and 4, AGAINST PROPOSAL 5, AND AS SAID PROXIES DEEM ADVISABLE
ON SUCH OTHER MATTERS AS MAY PROPERLY COME BEFORE THE MEETING AND ANY
POSTPONEMENTS OR ADJOURNMENTS THEREOF.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">PLEASE VOTE, SIGN, DATE AND
RETURN THIS PROXY CARD PROMPTLY USING THE ENCLOSED ENVELOPE OR VOTE THROUGH THE
INTERNET.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">IMPORTANT - TO BE SIGNED AND

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">VOTE BY INTERNET</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Dear Shareholder:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We are pleased to announce that you can now
vote your shares over the Internet. We encourage you to take advantage of this
new feature which eliminates the need to return the proxy card. Your Internet
vote is quick, convenient and your vote is immediately submitted. Just follow
these easy steps:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="border-collapse:collapse;width:100.0%;">
 <tr>

  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" color="white" face="Times New Roman" style="color:white;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">To vote using the Internet</font></b></p>
  </td>
  <td width="50%" valign="top" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:50.0%;">
  <p style="font-size:1.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;">&nbsp;</p>
  </td>
 </tr>

<p style="font-size:12.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .4in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.4in;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>&#149;&#160; <font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Go to the following
web site:<br>
<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">WWW.COMPUTERSHARE.COM/US/PROXY</font></b></font></p>

<p style="font-size:12.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .4in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.4in;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>&#149;&#160; <font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Enter the
information requested on your computer screen and follow the<br>
simple instructions.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Your Internet vote authorizes the named
proxies to vote your shares to the same extent as if you marked, signed, dated
and returned the proxy card. Please note that all votes cast by Internet must
be submitted prior to 12:00&nbsp;a.m. Central Time, April&nbsp;23, 2003.</font></p>

  Take the De Anza Blvd. exit<br>
  Make a right onto De Anza Blvd. (at signal)<br>
  Make a left onto Mariani Avenue<br>
  Enter Infinite Loop Parking Lot at the end<br>
  of Mariani Avenue<br>
  Proceed to Building 4</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="14%" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:14.48%;">
  <p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">[MAP]</font></b></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

Meeting is limited to shareholders. Admission to the meeting will be on a
first-come, first-served basis. In the interest of saving time and money, Apple
has opted to provide you with the enclosed Form 10-K for 2002 in lieu of
producing a glossy annual report.</font></p>
